< text>
Been coming here a couple times a month since 2014, when I used to work in the same shopping center. In my 6+ years of coming here, they have never messed up an order and I have never gotten sick. The quality is amazing compared to most sushi places in OC that I've been to. I've tried a majority of the items on the menu over the years; the volcano roll and super philly roll remain my favorites. Before COVID (when you could dine-in) they gave you complimentary miso soup and edamame. Definitely try this place out - you can't beat the quality for the price! No matter how busy they are - they always greet you, confirm your order with you, and the sushi chefs thank you as you leave. Thank you Kyotori for always being a reliable and satisfactory place for my sushi cravings! Keep up the great work! :)</text>

< Text>
I came through Chester on a recent trip to Northern California and was surprised to see a Dutch name on the sign across the road from the gas station I stopped at. I decided to check out this place and had one of their pastries. As a Dutch person I can attest that these pastries were really well done, very authentic, and they tasted great! The owners are also incredibly nice, and the wifi is reliable and fast. Definitely recommend this place if you're interested in some pastries, a hot beverage, and maybe even lunch (though I didn't try that). < Review>
This is my favorite restaurant, by far.  Their menu is varied; any selection lands you a tasty meal.  For lunch try the Tuna Manhattan *heavenly*, or the shrimp salad.  Whatever you choose, you won't be disappointed!  The atmosphere is welcoming, the wait staff are engaging.  This is a must-visit when you are in Auburn.</Review>

< text>
The only thing good about The Daily Egg,  and I mean GOOD. .not great,  not excellent, is the good.  The menu was good,  food was prepared well,  but took 15 minutes to have a server come take our order. Biscuits and gravy were cold and inedible, not that my appetite was all that great in the first place since the table next to ours (which had no diners at it) was filthy and never bussed the whole time we were there, very unappetizing. Would highly suggest bussing tables in a timely manner,  and not making customers who aren't regulars feel forgotten .</text>

Such a good place to eat.  Hard to find as it's in an industrial strip mall, but when you do find it you won't be disappointed.  Some of the best BBQ around.  Try their sandwich sampler so you can try different meats and find your favorite.  What is surprising was to me their turkey sandwich is excellent.  I would have thought the beef would have been the best, but the turkey was so good.  I've yet to have a bad thing from this place.  They also want to make sure they are doing good and check on you to make sure.  Definitely check this place out.  I've posted the current menu so you can get prices.  They are in the pricey side, but it's quality BBQ in a casual setting.  Much better than chain places like Dickie's.< /Review>

<pictures>None< /pictures><review>This an awesome place to experience great barbecue made by hard working salt of the earth people!  I am talking about real food, like fresh baked beans stewed with chunks of barbecued pork, not canned.  The Coleslaw was fresh, and I loved the celery seed seasoning to give it that extra fresh flavor.  And the barbecue...well, you'll have to experience the tender fall apart brisket and flavorful ribs.  Even their spicy barbecue sauce was good, with a nice kick, but not too much heat to scare off most timid diners.  The establishment was very clean and the service welcoming. One thing to note is that their diet soda selection was out of order on my visit.  Overall, a rare reasonably priced find, that I hope will continue to prosper in this out of the way industrial sector!< /review><Rate>5</Rate>< user_name>

< text>
We never anticipated finding such delicious and reasonably priced food in the area. They're located in an industrial park but easily viewable from the street. If you're a BBQ lover, you're in for a treat. They offer a huge variety of food, and so far we've tried their tender, fall off the bone, ribs, pastrami, pulled pork, pork roast, homemade mac and cheese, baked beans, and their cookies. We have yet to be disappointed! They're in the mix an amazing staff that is friendly, helpful and makes you feel like family from your first visit, and you have yourself a winning location to dine at.

Something to keep in mind if visiting with a larger group is that you'll easily fit on the patio, but the inside is on the smaller side with only about 12 tables that are mostly 4-tops. So plan accordingly.<//text>

<GmapID>0x80dcd68d971c2551:0x8da563562c17d50a<//GmapID>< user_name>

<Pics>None<//Pics></record></dataset><record>
<Rating>4<//Rating><Name>Joel Jervis<//Name><Gmap_id>0x80dcd68d971c2551:0x8da563562c17d50a</Gmap_id><pictures>None</pictures>< review>
I'm a fan.  Not the 'greatest' per say but still some really kind grinds.
I went with a friend and she recommended that I try the "Beef Brisket Sandwich" (sliced brisket, BBQ sauce, red onion and a sliced pickle on a French roll). @  $7.80
Instead I decided to order the "Pork Loin Sandwich" (sliced pork, BBQ sauce, onion, a sliced pickle on a French roll).@  $7.80
We split the Blake's Rings and French Fries combo: @ $5

So the experience we had was that this place was pretty crowded.  There was this guy sporting the coolest handlebar mustache; which I haven't seen in a long time. He took our order. We sat outside and our order came out rather quickly. The food runner was way nice and friendly.  While we were approximately half way through our meal another food runner going table to table asking about our experience.
Environment wise: Pretty cool: Plenty of seating inside and on the patio. TV's were set to sports channels and staff was super friendly.
Food wise: The  "Pork Loin Sandwich" was way to dry and I had to add BBQ sauce to help try and wet it up. Might've came in to order this on the wrong day.
Thank goodness I gave half of my sandwich to my friend and she gave me half of hers.  Her sandwich was GREAT!  I should've listened to her : /
The Onion Rings and French Fries were good.  The Onions rings were better since the fries came out a bit on the dry side and had to try and salvage them by the savior known as "Ketchup"

So here it is in a nutshell: Try the "Beef Brisket Sandwich"</review>

<Text>The Pulled Pork is exactly what it sounds like. It‚Äôs tender, slow-cooked, smoked pork that literally falls apart into shreds. They toss it in Blake‚Äôs BBQ sauce and serve it up in a lump. It has a little too much BBQ sauce for me. I‚Äôm more of a smoked meat person who uses the sauce on the side to add as needed. Otherwise, the pork tasted pretty good. Thumbs up!

Blake‚Äôs Big Pulled Pork Pile is slow smoked pork, pulled and served on their big bun with BBQ sauce, cole slaw, and red onion. You‚Äôll definitely need extra napkins for this sandwich! Again, a little too much BBQ sauce for me, but my family loved this sandwich! The sweet, BBQ sauced smoky pork complemented the cool, creamy cole slaw. The bun was soft yet held this pork beast together. Thumbs up! If you‚Äôre feeling a bit of Man vs. Food hunger, they also offer the Blake‚Äôs One Pounder Bomber or ‚ÄúTHE BEAST‚Äù (two and a half pounds of food, YIKES!)

Sandy‚Äôs Bread Pudding is a huge portion with a side of vanilla sauce to slather on. It was a very dense and custardy bread pudding. It had a bit more raisins in it than expected.
